              <script>
               (function($) {
 $(function() {
 
 var root = $('#j-carousel');
 var carouselInstance = null;
 
 
 $('.play-video', root).on('click', function(e) {
     e.preventDefault();
 
     var videoSrc = $(this).data('file');
     var videoType = $(this).data('type');
   	var playerWrapper = $('<div class="player-wrapper" tabindex="0" style="display:none; position:absolute; left:0; right:0; top:0; bottom:0; z-index:10000; background:#000; overflow:hidden"><a href="javascript:void(0)" class="close" style="position:absolute; right:10px; top:10px; z-index:2; display:block; width:28px; height:28px; cursor:pointer; text-indent:-9999px; background:url(/info/images/close.png) no-repeat 0 0">Close Video</a></div>');
   	
 	if (carouselInstance) {
 		carouselInstance.stop();
 	}    
     playerWrapper.appendTo(root).show().focus();  
     var playerHeight = playerWrapper.outerHeight();
     var playerWidth = playerWrapper.outerWidth();
     
     if (videoType == "youtube") {
 	    var playerEl = $('<iframe id="player" type="text/html" width="'+ playerWidth +'" height="' + playerHeight + '" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/' + videoSrc + '?enablejsapi=1&origin=http://www.wsulancers.com&autoplay=1&cc_load_policy=1&rel=0" frameborder="0"></iframe>')
         playerWrapper.append(playerEl);	    
     } else {
         var playerEl = $('<video/>').attr({
             'class': 'player video-js',
             'data-setup': '{"controls": true, "autoplay": true, "width":' + playerWidth + ', "height":' + playerHeight + '}'       
         });
         
         playerEl.append('<source src="' + videoSrc + '" type="' + videoType + '"  />');
         playerWrapper.append(playerEl);
         videojs($('.video-js', root).get(0));
     }
     $(document).trigger('dom_updated');
     
     videoFlag = true;
 });
 
 $('.seat.video', root).on('click', function(e) {
 	var seat = $(this);
 	if ($(e.target).is('.slide-img img')) {
 		e.preventDefault();
 		$('.play-video', seat).trigger('click');
 	}
 });
 
 root.on('click', '.close', function(e) {
     e.preventDefault();
 	if (carouselInstance) {
 		carouselInstance.play();
 	} 
 	
 	videoFlag = null;
 	
 	if ($('.video-js', root).length) {
     	videojs($('.video-js', root).get(0)).dispose(); 
 	}
     $('.player-wrapper', root).remove();
     $('.seat.active .play-video', root).focus();
 });
 
 $('.gallery', root).on('mouseenter', function() {
 	if (carouselInstance) {
 		carouselInstance.stop();
 	} 
 });
 
 $('.gallery', root).on('mouseleave', function() {
 	if (carouselInstance && !videoFlag) {
 		carouselInstance.play();
 	} 
 });
 
 carouselInstance = root.presto_Carousel(1000, 540, {
 	auto: true,
 	animation: 3, 
 	interval: 5000, 
 	animationSpeed: 400,
 	control: '.control'
 }).getPRESTO_Carousel();
 
 
 });
 })(jQuery);
              </script>

               $(function() {
   var carouselApi = $('#j-carousel').getPRESTO_Carousel()
   var controls = $('#carousel-content').children('.content');
 
   $('#j-carousel').on('beforeSlide', function(e, activeIndex, lastIndex) {
 
     if (lastIndex >= 0) {
       controls.eq(lastIndex).removeClass('active');
     }
     controls.eq(activeIndex).addClass('active');
 
   });
 
 });

              <section class="sect-aotw">
               <h2 class="sect-hdr">
                Lancer Spotlight
               </h2>
               <div class="aotw clearfix">
                <div class="athlete clearfix">
                 <a class="thumb" href="/sports/mtrack-out/2017-18/releases/MTF053018">
                  <img alt="" src="/sports/mtrack-out/2017-18/photos/JL.jpg?max_width=260"/>
                 </a>
                 <div class="info">
                  <a class="title" href="/sports/mtrack-out/2017-18/releases/MTF053018">
                   <span>
                    Lewis’ Back-to-Back National Championships Earns Him MASCAC Field Athlete of the Week Honors
                   </span>
                  </a>
                  <span class="leadin">
                   WORCESTER, Mass. – Worcester State University’s Justin Lewis (Lynn, Mass.) has been named the Massachusetts State Collegiate Athletic Conference (MASCAC) field athlete of the week following earning back-to-back outdoor high jump championships at the NCAA DIII Outdoor Track &amp; Field Championships.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                </div>
                <div class="athlete clearfix">
                 <a class="thumb" href="/sports/wtrack-out/2017-18/releases/WTF052318">
                  <img alt="" src="/sports/wtrack-out/2017-18/photos/Action_Photos/Bernice_Mensah_4.jpg?max_width=260"/>
                 </a>
                 <div class="info">
                  <a class="title" href="/sports/wtrack-out/2017-18/releases/WTF052318">
                   <span>
                    Mensah Captures Final MASCAC Women’s Outdoor Track &amp; Field Rookie of the Week Award
                   </span>
                  </a>
                  <span class="leadin">
                   WORCESTER, Mass. – Worcester State University’s Bernice Mensah (Worcester, Mass.) has earned the final Massachusetts State Collegiate Athletic Conference (MASCAC) women’s outdoor track &amp; field rookie of the week accolade.
                  </span>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>

                Previous Athletes
               </a>

         <script>
          (function($) {
 $(function() {
 
 var api;
 var root = $('#main-tabs');
 var tabs = root.children('.tabs');
 var panes = root.children('.panes').children('.pane');
 var tabTitles = root.children('.panes').children('.tab_title[data-tab]');
 
 api = tabs.tabs(panes, {
     current: 'active',
 	tabs: 'a[data-tab]',
     initialIndex: 0,
     onBeforeClick: function(e, i) {
         tabs.removeClass('state' + (this.getIndex() + 1)).addClass('state' + (i + 1));
         tabTitles.removeClass('active').eq(i).addClass('active');
         panes.removeClass('active').eq(i).addClass('active');
     },
 	onClick: function() {
 		$(document).trigger("ui_updated");
 	}
 }).data('tabConfig', { 'initialIndex': 0 }).data('tabs');
 
 tabTitles.click(function(e) {
   e.preventDefault();
   if (typeof api !== 'undefined') {
     api.click(tabTitles.index(this));
   }
 });
 
 });
 })(jQuery);
         </script>
